</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="least" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">least<a class="headerlink" href="#least" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns the smaller value of a and b.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">least(a, b)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="greatest" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">greatest<a class="headerlink" href="#greatest" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns the larger value of a and b.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">greatest(a, b)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="blocknumber" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">blockNumber<a class="headerlink" href="#blocknumber" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns a monotonically increasing sequence number of the block containing the row.<!-- --> <!-- -->The returned block number is updated on a best-effort basis, i.e. it may not be fully accurate.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">blockNumber()
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>Sequence number of the data block where the row is located. UInt64.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT blockNumber()
FROM
(
    SELECT *
    FROM system.numbers
    LIMIT 10
) SETTINGS max_block_size = 2
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─blockNumber()─┐

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>Ordinal number of the row in the data block starting from 0. UInt64.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT rowNumberInBlock()
FROM
(
    SELECT *
    FROM system.numbers_mt
    LIMIT 10
) SETTINGS max_block_size = 2
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─rowNumberInBlock()─┐
│                  0 │
│                  1 │
└────────────────────┘

│                  0 │
│                  1 │

│                  0 │

└────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="rownumberinallblocks" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">rowNumberInAllBlocks<a class="headerlink" href="#rownumberinallblocks" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns a unique row number for each row processed by <code>rowNumberInAllBlocks</code>. The returned numbers start at 0.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">rowNumberInAllBlocks()
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>Ordinal number of the row in the data block starting from 0. UInt64.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT rowNumberInAllBlocks()
FROM
(
    SELECT *
    FROM system.numbers_mt
    LIMIT 10
)
SETTINGS max_block_size = 2
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─rowNumberInAllBlocks()─┐
│                      0 │
│                      1 │
└────────────────────────┘
┌─rowNumberInAllBlocks()─┐
│                      4 │
│                      5 │
└────────────────────────┘
┌─rowNumberInAllBlocks()─┐
│                      2 │
│                      3 │
└────────────────────────┘
┌─rowNumberInAllBlocks()─┐
│                      6 │
│                      7 │
└────────────────────────┘
┌─rowNumberInAllBlocks()─┐
│                      8 │
│                      9 │
└────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="neighbor" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">neighbor<a class="headerlink" href="#neighbor" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>The window function that provides access to a row at a specified offset before or after the current row of a given column.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">neighbor(column, offset[, default_value])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>The result of the function depends on the affected data blocks and the order of data in the block.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Only returns neighbor inside the currently processed data block.<!-- --> <!-- -->Because of this error-prone behavior the function is DEPRECATED, please use proper window functions instead.</p></div></div><p>The order of rows during calculation of <code>neighbor()</code> can differ from the order of rows returned to the user.<!-- --> <!-- -->To prevent that you can create a subquery with ORDER BY and call the function from outside the subquery.</p><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>column</code>: A column name or scalar expression.</li><li><code>offset</code>: The number of rows to look before or ahead of the current row in <code>column</code>. Int64.</li><li><code>default_value</code>: Optional. The returned value if offset is beyond the block boundaries. Type of data blocks affected.</li></ul><h3 id="returned-values" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned values<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-values" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>Value of <code>column</code> with <code>offset</code> distance from current row, if <code>offset</code> isn&#x27;t outside the block boundaries.</li><li>The default value of <code>column</code> or <code>default_value</code> (if given), if <code>offset</code> is outside the block boundaries.</li></ul><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>The return type will be that of the data blocks affected or the default value type.</p></div></div><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT number, neighbor(number, 2) FROM system.numbers LIMIT 10
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─number─┬─neighbor(number, 2)─┐
│      0 │                   2 │
│      1 │                   3 │
│      2 │                   4 │
│      3 │                   5 │
│      4 │                   6 │
│      5 │                   7 │
│      6 │                   8 │
│      7 │                   9 │
│      8 │                   0 │
│      9 │                   0 │
└────────┴─────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT number, neighbor(number, 2, 999) FROM system.numbers LIMIT 10
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─number─┬─neighbor(number, 2, 999)─┐
│      0 │                        2 │
│      1 │                        3 │
│      2 │                        4 │
│      3 │                        5 │
│      4 │                        6 │
│      5 │                        7 │
│      6 │                        8 │
│      7 │                        9 │
│      8 │                      999 │
│      9 │                      999 │
└────────┴──────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This function can be used to compute year-over-year metric value:</p><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">WITH toDate(&#x27;2018-01-01&#x27;) AS start_date
SELECT
    toStartOfMonth(start_date + (number * 32)) AS month,
    toInt32(month) % 100 AS money,
    neighbor(money, -12) AS prev_year,
    round(prev_year / money, 2) AS year_over_year
FROM numbers(16)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌──────month─┬─money─┬─prev_year─┬─year_over_year─┐
│ 2018-01-01 │    32 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-02-01 │    63 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-03-01 │    91 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-04-01 │    22 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-05-01 │    52 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-06-01 │    83 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-07-01 │    13 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-08-01 │    44 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-09-01 │    75 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-10-01 │     5 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-11-01 │    36 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2018-12-01 │    66 │         0 │              0 │
│ 2019-01-01 │    97 │        32 │           0.33 │
│ 2019-02-01 │    28 │        63 │           2.25 │
│ 2019-03-01 │    56 │        91 │           1.62 │
│ 2019-04-01 │    87 │        22 │           0.25 │
└────────────┴───────┴───────────┴────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="runningdifference" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">runningDifference<a class="headerlink" href="#runningdifference" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Calculates the difference between two consecutive row values in the data block.<!-- --> <!-- -->Returns 0 for the first row, and for subsequent rows the difference to the previous row.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Only returns differences inside the currently processed data block.<!-- --> <!-- -->Because of this error-prone behavior the function is DEPRECATED, please use proper window functions instead.</p></div></div><p>The result of the function depends on the affected data blocks and the order of data in the block.</p><p>The order of rows during calculation of <code>runningDifference()</code> can differ from the order of rows returned to the user.<!-- --> <!-- -->To prevent that you can create a subquery with ORDER BY and call the function from outside the subquery.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">runningDifference(x)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    EventID,
    EventTime,
    runningDifference(EventTime) AS delta
FROM
(
    SELECT
        EventID,
        EventTime
    FROM events
    WHERE EventDate = &#x27;2016-11-24&#x27;
    ORDER BY EventTime ASC
    LIMIT 5
)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─EventID─┬───────────EventTime─┬─delta─┐
│    1106 │ 2016-11-24 00:00:04 │     0 │
│    1107 │ 2016-11-24 00:00:05 │     1 │
│    1108 │ 2016-11-24 00:00:05 │     0 │
│    1109 │ 2016-11-24 00:00:09 │     4 │
│    1110 │ 2016-11-24 00:00:10 │     1 │
└─────────┴─────────────────────┴───────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Please note that the block size affects the result. The internal state of <code>runningDifference</code> state is reset for each new block.</p><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    number,
    runningDifference(number + 1) AS diff
FROM numbers(100000)
WHERE diff != 1
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─number─┬─diff─┐
│      0 │    0 │
└────────┴──────┘
┌─number─┬─diff─┐
│  65536 │    0 │
└────────┴──────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">set max_block_size=100000 -- default value is 65536!

SELECT
    number,
    runningDifference(number + 1) AS diff
FROM numbers(100000)
WHERE diff != 1
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─number─┬─diff─┐
│      0 │    0 │
└────────┴──────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="runningdifferencestartingwithfirstvalue" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">runningDifferenceStartingWithFirstValue<a class="headerlink" href="#runningdifferencestartingwithfirstvalue" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>This function is DEPRECATED (see the note for <code>runningDifference</code>).</p></div></div><p>Same as runningDifference, but returns the value of the first row as the value on the first row.</p><h2 id="runningconcurrency" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">runningConcurrency<a class="headerlink" href="#runningconcurrency" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Calculates the number of concurrent events.<!-- --> <!-- -->Each event has a start time and an end time. The start time is included in the event, while the end time is excluded. Columns with a start time and an end time must be of the same data type.<!-- --> <!-- -->The function calculates the total number of active (concurrent) events for each event start time.</p><p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"></div></div>tip<!-- --> <!-- -->Events must be ordered by the start time in ascending order. If this requirement is violated the function raises an exception. Every data block is processed separately. If events from different data blocks overlap then they can&#x27;t be processed correctly.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"></div></div><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">runningConcurrency(start, end)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>start</code>: A column with the start time of events. Date, DateTime, or DateTime64.</li><li><code>end</code>: A column with the end time of events. Date, DateTime, or DateTime64.</li></ul><h3 id="returned-values" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned values<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-values" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>The number of concurrent events at each event start time. UInt32</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Consider the table:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌──────start─┬────────end─┐
│ 2021-03-03 │ 2021-03-11 │
│ 2021-03-06 │ 2021-03-12 │
│ 2021-03-07 │ 2021-03-08 │
│ 2021-03-11 │ 2021-03-12 │
└────────────┴────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT start, runningConcurrency(start, end) FROM example_table

Returns the corresponding MAC address in format AA:BB:CC:DD:EE:FF (colon-separated numbers in hexadecimal form) as string.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">MACNumToString(num)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="macstringtonum" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">MACStringToNum<a class="headerlink" href="#macstringtonum" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>The inverse function of MACNumToString. If the MAC address has an invalid format, it returns 0.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">MACStringToNum(s)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="macstringtooui" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">MACStringToOUI<a class="headerlink" href="#macstringtooui" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Given a MAC address in format AA:BB:CC:DD:EE:FF (colon-separated numbers in hexadecimal form), returns the first three octets as a UInt64 number. If the MAC address has an invalid format, it returns 0.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">MACStringToOUI(s)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="getsizeofenumtype" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">getSizeOfEnumType<a class="headerlink" href="#getsizeofenumtype" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns the number of fields in Enum.<!-- --> <!-- -->An exception is thrown if the type isn&#x27;t <code>Enum</code>.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">getSizeOfEnumType(value)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>value</code>: Value of type <code>Enum</code>.</li></ul><h3 id="returned-values" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned values<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-values" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>The number of fields with <code>Enum</code> input values.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT getSizeOfEnumType( CAST(&#x27;a&#x27; AS Enum8(&#x27;a&#x27; = 1, &#x27;b&#x27; = 2) ) ) AS x

│ 2 │
└───┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="blockserializedsize" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">blockSerializedSize<a class="headerlink" href="#blockserializedsize" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns the size on disk without considering compression.</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">blockSerializedSize(value[, value[, ...]])

fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT dumpColumnStructure(CAST(&#x27;2018-01-01 01:02:03&#x27;, &#x27;DateTime&#x27;))
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─dumpColumnStructure(CAST(&#x27;2018-01-01 01:02:03&#x27;, &#x27;DateTime&#x27;))─┐
│ DateTime, Const(size = 1, UInt32(size = 1))                  │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 arrayJoin.</p></div></div><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" </pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>x</code>: The value to fill the result array with.</li><li><code>arr</code>: An array. Array.</li></ul><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>An array of the lame length as <code>arr</code> filled with value <code>x</code>. Array.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT replicate(1, [&#x27;a&#x27;, &#x27;b&#x27;, &#x27;c&#x27;])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─replicate(1, [&#x27;a&#x27;, &#x27;b&#x27;, &#x27;c&#x27;])─┐

└───────────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="initializeaggregation" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">initializeAggregation<a class="headerlink" href="#initializeaggregation" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Calculates the result of an aggregate function based on a single value. This function can be used to initialize aggregate functions with combinator -State. You can create states of aggregate functions and insert them to columns of type AggregateFunction or use initialized aggregates as default values.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">initializeAggregation (aggregate_function, arg1, arg2, ..., argN)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>aggregate_function</code>: Name of the aggregation function to initialize. String.</li><li><code>arg</code>: Arguments of aggregate function.</li></ul><h3 id="returned-values" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned values<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-values" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>Result of aggregation for every row passed to the function.</li></ul><p>The return type is the same as the return type of function, that <code>initializeAggregation</code> takes as first argument.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT uniqMerge(state) FROM (SELECT initializeAggregation(&#x27;uniqState&#x27;, number % 3) AS state FROM numbers(10000))
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─uniqMerge(state)─┐
│                3 │
└──────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT finalizeAggregation(state), toTypeName(state) FROM (SELECT initializeAggregation(&#x27;sumState&#x27;, number % 3) AS state FROM numbers(5))
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─finalizeAggregation(state)─┬─toTypeName(state)─────────────┐
